***thermodynamica.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thermodynamica.html>thermodynamica</a> (98781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thermodynamics</i>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thermodynamica.html>thermodynamica</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>thermodynamics</li></ol>

***theta.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:theta.html>theta</a> (42956)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θῆτα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thêta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:theta.html>theta</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thetas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The eighth letter of the Modern Greek alphabet, ninth in Old Greek: Θ, θ.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The measure of an angle.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The sensitivity of the value of a derivative with respect to time; the "time decay".</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Designating a level of brain activity as measured by electroencephalography having a frequency of between four and seven <a href = vnd.unilang:cycles.html>cycles</a> per second (associated with drowsiness in adults).
<ul><li><b>2018</b>, Meghan <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Gieblyn, "The Most Unread Book Ever Acclaimed", <i>The Paris Review</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theparisreview.org/blog/2018/09/19/the-most-unread-book-ever-acclaimed/">19 September</a>:
<dl><dd>The reader <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> less likely to throw the book down in a fit of disgust than she <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to be lulled into a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:theta.html>theta</a></b> state, a highway hypnosis induced by page after page of incantatory prose.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The voiceless dental fricative represented by θ.</li></ol>
</body>

***thom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> thom (18465)</h1><br></body> 
***thong.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a> (72455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">thwong</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">thwang</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þwong</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þwang</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þweng</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þwæng</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a>, strap, cord, strip of leather; phylactery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þwangiz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þwanguz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coercion, constraint, <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a>, clamp, strap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*twenk-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeeze, press, pressure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">thwang</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">thwayng</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">thang</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">dwenge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clamp, <a href = vnd.unilang:jaws.html>jaws</a>, steel-trap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zwinge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vise, clamp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">tveng</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shoestrap, shoelace</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">þvengur</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strap, <a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a>, latchet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thongs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A strip of leather.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An item of footwear, usually of rubber, secured by two straps which join to pass between the big <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a> and its neighbour.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1963</b> March 16,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hal_Porter" class="extiw" title="w:Hal Porter"><a href = vnd.unilang:hal.html>Hal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>Porter</a></a>,  “Little old lady passing by”, in  <cite>The Bulletin</cite>, page 22, column 3:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Because of August he wears <a href = vnd.unilang:shorts.html>shorts</a> and sandals, the Japanese <i>geta</i> sort called <b>thongs</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1964</b>, The Beach Boys, <i>All Summer Long</i>

***thor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thor.html>thor</a> (16766)</h1><br></body> 
***thorax.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thorax.html>thorax</a> (58976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:thorax.html>thorax</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θώραξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thṓrax</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a breastplate, cuirass, corslet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thorax.html>thorax</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thoraces</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thoraxes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The region of the mammalian body between the neck and abdomen as well as the cavity containing the heart and lungs.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology and arachnology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The middle of three distinct divisions in an insect, crustacean or arachnid body to which the <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> are attached.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:thorax.html>thorax</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:anatomie.html>anatomie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:borstkas.html>borstkas</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ribbenkast.html>ribbenkast</a>, borstholte</li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Afgeleide_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:afgeleide.html>Afgeleide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>thoraxchirurgie, thoraxfoto</li></ul>

***thuis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a> (278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">thuus</i>, contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> huus</i>; equivalent to modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>at home <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">at one's dwelling or in one's home area</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm not <b>at home</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They're not <b>home</b> yet.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voel.html>voel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I feel <b>at home</b> around here.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>one's home</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thuishoren.html>thuishoren</a> (22997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thuishoren.html>thuishoren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to belong, to be in one's preferred or appropriate place

***thunderbolt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thunderbolt.html>thunderbolt</a> (67126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thunder</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bolt</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thunderbolt.html>thunderbolt</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thunderbolts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A flash of lightning accompanied by a crash of thunder.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An event that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> terrible, horrific or unexpected.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1697</b>,  “<span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(please specify the book number)</span>”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="w:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, transl., <cite>The Works of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virgil" class="extiw" title="w:Virgil"><a href = vnd.unilang:virgil.html>Virgil</a></a>: Containing His Pastorals, Georgics, and Æneis.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Translated into English Verse; by Mr. DRYDEN. Adorn’d with a Hundred Sculptures.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, London |  Printed for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacob_Tonson" class="extiw" title="w:Jacob Tonson"><a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Tonson</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Judges Head in Fleetstreet, near the Inner-Temple-Gate.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/403869432">403869432</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>the Scipios' worth, those <b>thunderbolts</b> of war</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Vehement threatening or censure; especially, ecclesiastical denunciation; fulmination.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Hakewill and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>He severely threatens such with the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thunderbolt.html>thunderbolt</a></b> of excommunication.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">soccer</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A very powerful shot.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> February 5,  Michael Kevin Darling,  “Tottenham 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 1 Bolton”, in  <cite>BBC</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/9382905.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Substitute <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Niko_Kranjcar" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Niko Kranjcar"><a href = vnd.unilang:niko.html>Niko</a> Kranjcar</a>'s injury-time <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thunderbolt.html>thunderbolt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> Tottenham a dramatic win <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> Bolton.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">paleontology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A belemnite, or thunderstone.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A charge in the form of two joined bundles with four <a href = vnd.unilang:rays.html>rays</a> of lightning emerging from them, resembling the <a href = vnd.unilang:thunderbolt.html>thunderbolt</a> of Jupiter.</li>
<li>A daring or irresistible hero.</li></ol>
</body>

***thwaite.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thwaite.html>thwaite</a> (62699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*thwait</i>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">þveit</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">paddock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">þveita</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hurl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">whittle</i>), Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">døjt</i> (“<small><sup>1</sup><big>⁄</big><sub>160</sub></small> of the gulden”, dialectal: “a small coin”), German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Deut</i>, Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duit.html>duit</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þwītan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to thwite; cut; cut off</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">doit</i>, and possibly of <i><span class="Latn" lang="en">twat</span></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thwaite.html>thwaite</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thwaites</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of forest <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> cleared for agriculture or habitation; a clearing; assart</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">thwite</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">twaite</i></span></span></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:tic.html>tic</a></i>

***tief.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a> (87359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">tiuf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">tiuf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*deupaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰewb-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">deep</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diep.html>diep</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deep</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">dyb</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">dyp</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">djúpur</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de">tiefer</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am tiefsten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deep (also figuratively)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a></b> ist <a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>das</a> Wasser?</i>
<dl><dd>How deep <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the water?</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:sie.html>Sie</a> hat ein <b>tiefes</b> Verständnis <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> russischen Kultur.</i>
<dl><dd>She <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a deep understanding of Russian culture.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>low
<dl><dd><i>Du hast <a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>das</a> Bild zu <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a></b> gehängt.</i>
<dl><dd>You hung the picture too low.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">niedrig</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a more generally applicable translation of English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">low</i>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>Tief</a></i> can cover the meaning of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">niedrig</i> in many contexts, but not vice versa.
</p>
</body>

***tieren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tieren.html>tieren</a> (36571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tieren.html>tieren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*tiari-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">neat, splendid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*DiH-or-i-</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>  The ultimate origin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> uncertain, but cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">tærr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clear (water)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which could be related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">tár</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> lt;lt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tahrą</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zieren</i>, and also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sieren.html>sieren</a></i> which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from Middle High German.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tieren.html>tieren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to thrive, prosper</li>
<li>to make a fuss, to rant</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tiet.html>tiet</a> (13431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Titte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nipple; breast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*titt-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">teat; nipple; breast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tata-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">father; parent; nipple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zitze</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tit</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">teat</i>.

***tig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tig.html>tig</a> (17566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-tig</i> used to form multiples of ten.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tig.html>tig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tens, dozens, lots
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tig.html>tig</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:redenen.html>redenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedenken.html>bedenken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarom.html>waarom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fout.html>fout</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>!</i>
<dl><dd>I can think of <b>dozens</b> of reasons why this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> wrong!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr />

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schrift.html>schrift</a></i>, in the senses “magazine” probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zeitschrift</i>.

<ol><li>magazine <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">periodical of which print instalments appear</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
